157a2(mdo sde2): lag brgyad pa mngon du gyur te/ zad pa thams cad bcad nas/ sdug bsngal gyi mtha' zad par byed do// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen po 'jig
157a3(mdo sde2): rten du shar ba na lo tog thams cad skye zhing 'phel te/ me tog dang / lo ma thams cad rgyas pa dang / mnam zhing brtsog pa thams cad sel ba dang / lo tog gi 'bru dang /
157a4(mdo sde2): sman gyi 'bras bu thams cad smin pa dang / gangs kyi ri 'o kun zhu bas 'bab chu kun 'brug ste/ rims kyis rgya mtsho chen por 'bab par 'gyur ro// de bzhin du byang chub
157a5(mdo sde2): sems dpa'i sems dpa' chen po yang 'khor lo rnam pa 'di bcu dang ldan te/ lhag pa'i sbyin pa la gshing dul ba'i tshul khrims dang / bde ba'i bzod pa dang / brtson
157a6(mdo sde2): 'grus dang / bsam gtan dang / shes rab dang / thabs dang / byams pa dang / snying rje dang / spobs pa'i yon tan shin du rgyas zhing sems can thams cad la dam pa'i
157a7(mdo sde2): chos ston to// chos de'i 'od kyi gzi brjid kyis sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba lhag pa'i lo tog rnam pa sna tshogs skye zhing 'phel ba dang / lhag pa'i spyod
157a8(mdo sde2): pa dam pa'i me tog dang / lo ma rnam pa sna tshogs shin du rgyas pa dang / nyon mongs pa'i las ngan pa thams cad yongs su sel ba dang / mtho ris dang mya ngan las 'da'
157b1(mdo sde2): theg pa gcig pu bshad// da lta'i 'khor 'di theg pa gsum snod can// la la nyan thos theg pa'i chos dang ldan// las kyi dngos po mang pos 'jigs pa dag/ de ni byang chub mchog
157b2(mdo sde2): gi snod ma yin// la la dben par dga' zhing rang byang chub/ de yang byang chub mchog gi snod ma yin// la la ye shes mchog la dkod 'os pa// de bas mos pa bzhin du theg gsuM
157b3(mdo sde2): shod// sbyangs pa'i yon tan gyis ni grol 'dod pa// theg chen bshad pa thos na ngan song lhung // bad ken nad la 'o ma 'thung bcug bzhin// de phyir dug du 'gyur gyi nad mi sel//
157b4(mdo sde2): de bzhin snod min nyan thos theg pa dag/ theg chen bshad pa thos na rmongs 'gyur zhing // chad par lta la ngan song lhung 'gyur bas// de bas dbang po brtags te chos bstan
157b5(mdo sde2): to// shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// sa'i snying po'i 'khor lo bcu pa zhes bya ba las gnas pa dang spyad pa'i le'u ste// / bzhi pa'o// /
157b6(mdo sde2): de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyis tshigs su bcad pa de dag gsungs pa na/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de'i nang na sems can tshad med pa brgya stong snyed/ sngon chos thos pa las
157b7(mdo sde2): yi gol te stong pa yin par go nas/ rgyu dang 'bras bu med par lta zhing / dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bcad nas/ ngan song du ltung bar 'gyur ba dag mdo sde 'di bshad pa
157b8(mdo sde2): thos nas phyir yang / yang dag pa'i lte ba dang ldan par gyur to// de nas de dag 'dug pa las langs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar shin tu mdzes pa bskyed de/
139a1(mdo sde2): so sor bshags par bya ba'i phyir/ thal mo sbyar ba btud te phyag 'tshal nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// btsun
139a2(mdo sde2): pa bcom ldan 'das bdag cag sngon nyan thos kyi theg pa pa'i rigs su dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa las/ nyan thos kyi theg pa'i rigs su dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa las nyan thos
139a3(mdo sde2): kyi theg pa de yang yongs su smin par sangs rgyas kyi chos thos so// de la'ang rmongs shing mngon du ma gyur pas/ stong par lta zhing rgyu dang 'bras bu yang med par yang 'dzin te/
139a4(mdo sde2): de'i rgyu de'i rkyen gyis lus dang ngag yid kyi sgo nas sdig pa mi dge ba'i las tshad med pa bgyis pas/ ngan song dag tu ltung bar 'gyur ba las/ dang bcom ldan 'das kyi
139a5(mdo sde2): spyan sngar mdo sde 'di bshad pa thos nas/ slar yang yang dag pa'i lta ba rnyed de shin tu 'dzem pa dang / ngo tsha ba'i sems kyis so sor bshags te/ ma bcabs pas de dag yod
139a6(mdo sde2): su byang bar gyur cig/ deng slan chad ji srid sgrib par 'gyur ba'i las rnams mi bgyid par yongs su bsrung bar 'tshal lo// bdag cag gi sdig pa de dag yongasu byang ba dang /
139a7(mdo sde2): slan cad mi bgyid par bcom ldan 'das thugs brtse bas rjes su gzung du gsol/ bdag cag ma 'ongs pa na ngan song gi sdug bsngal myong bar 'gyur ba las thugs brtse bas
139a8(mdo sde2): bskyang du gsol/ bdag cag slar yang sngon spyad pa'i nyan thos kyi theg pa la spyod cing nan tan bgyid kyis bcom ldan 'das thugs brtse ba'i slad du bstan du gsol/ bcom ldan
139b1(mdo sde2): ba'i 'bras bu yongs su smin par 'gyur ba dang / log par lta ba dang / nga rgyal gyi ri bo thams cad zhu zhing 'bab pas yang dag pa'i dad pa dang tshul khrims dang / thos pa
139b2(mdo sde2): dang / gtong ba dang / shes rab dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi chu rim gyis 'bab cing mya ngan las 'da' ba'i rgya mtsho 'gengs pa dang / sems can thams cad yid bzhin du
139b3(mdo sde2): 'jigs pa med pa mya ngan las 'da' ba'i grong khyer du 'jug par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu de la ji ltar na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i 'khor lo
139b4(mdo sde2): bcu gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'khor lo bcu pa zhes bya ba ni chos gzhan la mi gdags kyi/ dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam nyid yin par shes par bya'o// 'khor lo rnam pa
139b5(mdo sde2): bcu po 'di dag dang ldan pas ne/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po zhes bya ste/ sdig pa thams cad las rnam par grol ba dang / dge ba'i chos thams cad
139b6(mdo sde2): yid bzhin du rdzogs pa dang / myur du mya ngan las 'da' ba chen po'i rgya mtsho yongs su 'gengs pa dang / thabs mkhas pa chen po'i ye shes kyi
139b7(mdo sde2): 'od kyis skye bo thams cad yongasu smin par byed cing thams cad phan pa dang bde ba yongs su thob par byed do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi bu snga ma 'das pa'i sangs
139b8(mdo sde2): rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad kyis kyang mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam yongs su spangs te/ dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam 'di la yongasu bsngags pas 'bras bu
158a1(mdo sde2): thob par gyur to// de bas na dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bshad pa 'di dag las dga' zhing nam mtsho ba'i bar du ma nyams par srung na/
158a2(mdo sde2): 'bras bu khyad par can mchog tu 'gyur ba thams cad thob pa ni ji ltar bshad pa bzhin no// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang na
158a3(mdo sde2): mtsho'i bar du srog gcod pa yongs su spangs na/ de nyid sems can la mi 'jigs pa sbyin pa yin te/ sems can dag la 'jigs shing bag tsha bar mi byed pas de'i
158a4(mdo sde2): 'jigs pa'i sdug bsngal mi skyed pa'i dbang gis dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad myur du yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// thog ma med pa'i mtha' nas rgyud lngar 'khor lo
158a5(mdo sde2): 'khor ba'i rgya mtshor bying ba srog gcod pa'i dbang gis lus dang ngag dang yid kyis sdig pa mi dge ba'i las bdag kyang byed la gzhan yang byed du 'jug cing mthong ba
158a6(mdo sde2): dang thos pa'i rjes su yi rang ba las byung ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / sems can gyi sgrib pa dang / chos kyi sgrib pa dang / tshe'i sgrib pas bsgribs par gyur to//
158a7(mdo sde2): 'di ltar srog gcod pa yongs su spangs pa'i 'khor los de dag lhag ma ma lus par yongs su bcom zhing rnyil bas rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu mi myong bar byed do//
158a8(mdo sde2): las 'di nyid la yang lha dang mi la sogs pa kun dga' zhing yid du 'ong ba dang / dogs pa mi skye ba dang / lus dang sems las su bde zhing yun ring du 'tsho bar 'gyur ro// /
158b1(mdo sde2): 'chi 'pho ba'i dus byed pa na yang lus dang sems la sdug bsngal gyis mi gdung zhing yid du 'ong ba'i bu dang chung ma dang 'khor thams cad kyis yongs su bskor bas 'chi
158b2(mdo sde2): 'pho ba'i dus byed kyi/ shin du 'jigs pa gshin rje'i pho nya mthong bar mi 'gyur ro// gzhan yang yid du 'ong ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen chos kyis dul ba'i tshul
158b3(mdo sde2): khrims dang yon tan du ldan pa bsod nams kyi zhing yang dag pa dang phrad de/ lus dang sems rab du dga' ba dang / de la bkur sti dang / bcas pas shin tu dad
158b4(mdo sde2): pa skye bar 'gyur ro// yang tshe 'phos nas kyang phyir mi yi nang du skye ste/ dbang po yongs su rdzogs shing yan lag dang ldan pa dang / gang nas gang du skyes par nad
158b5(mdo sde2): med pa dang / tshe ring ba dang / byad gzugs bzang ba dang yid gzhungs pa dang / rab tu bde zhing skyid pa dang / gzhan yang yid du 'ong ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen
158b6(mdo sde2): chos kyis dul ba tshul khrims dang yon tan du ldan pa bsod nams kyi zhing yang dag pa dang phrad de/ de'i rjes su slob pa dang srog gcod pa yongs su spong ba dang / sdig
158b7(mdo sde2): pa mi dge ba'i chos thams cad yongs su spyod pa dang / dge ba'i chos khyed par can thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa dang / theg pa chen po'i chos kyi rnam grangs thams/
158b8(mdo sde2): cad tshol ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam dang / spyod pa thams cad la rim gyis gzhol zhing shin tu yangs pa'i ye shes kyi rgya mtsho la 'jug pa nas/ tha
159a1(mdo sde2): na med pa'i byang chub thob pa'i bar du 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi zhing mtshon cha med pa dang / dgra dang 'tshe ba'i ming mi grag pa dang / 'jigs
159a2(mdo sde2): pa thams cad dang bral te rab du bde skyid pa dang / nad med pa dang / tshe ring ba'i zhing du sems can dag skyed par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshe'i tshad kyang dpag
159a3(mdo sde2): tu med de/ sems can dag cis 'dul bzhin du dam pa'i chos ston to// yongs su mya ngan las 'das kyang dam pa'i chos yun ring du gnas shing / sems can
159a4(mdo sde2): tshad med pa la phan pa dang bde ba'i don byed par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po srog gcod pa yongs su spangs pa ste/
159a5(mdo sde2): 'khor lo ste dang po// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'khor lo de dang ldan na/ nyan thos kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur nyan thos kyi theg pa'i

159a7(mdo sde2): 'gyur ro// theg pa chen po la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur/ theg pa chen po'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung yongs su
159a8(mdo sde2): 'phel ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la rab du byung ba'i nye gnas kyi snod dam/ chos kyi snod ma yin pa yang rung / chung ngun chos gos kyi tshal bu gyon
159b1(mdo sde2): cing sgra dang kha spu bregs pa la/ 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// theg pa chen po'i chos la grong nas gong du 'phrar zhing phyir mi ldog pa dang / rno ba'i shes rab dang /
159b2(mdo sde2): bsod nams kyi khyad par rtag du skye zhing 'phel ba dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / gzungs dang / bzod pa dang sa rnams thams cad dbang du 'gyur zhing phyir mi ldog pa
159b3(mdo sde2): dang / rtag tu dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang phrad cing rjes su 'gro ba dang / rtag tu sangs rgyas thams cad mthong ba dang / mi 'bral zhing byang chub sems dpa' dang /

159b5(mdo sde2): ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad tshol ba la brtson pas sems mi ngoms pa dang / byang chub kyi spyod pa dang / smon lam rnam pa sna tshogs kyis sems mi ngom

159b8(mdo sde2): ba dang / bdag nyid tshul bzhin du snyed nor gyis chog shes par gnas kyi chos ma yin pa'i nor dang / khyi la re ba med pa de'i dbang gis dge ba'i rtsa ba thams

161a1(mdo sde2): ldan pa'i zhing der sems can dag skye bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshe'i tshad kyang dpag tu med de/ sems can dag ci 'dul/

162a1(mdo sde2): ba las byung ba nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / sems can gyi sgrib pa dang / chos kyi sgrib pa dang / chung ma'i sgrib pas sgribs par 'gyur ro//
162a2(mdo sde2): 'di ltar 'dod pas log par g.yem pa yongs su spangs pa'i 'khor los lhag ma ma lus par bcom pas rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu me len te/ lus 'di nyid la yang

169a1(mdo sde2): nyan cing gus pas dogs pa med par 'gyur ro// de'i dbang gis dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// thog ma
169a2(mdo sde2): med pa'i mtha' nas rgyud lngar 'khor bar 'khor ba'i rgya mtshor 'bying ba yang tshig kyal pa smras pa'i dbang gis lus dang ngag dang yid mi dge ba'i las bdag kyang byed la gzhan
169a3(mdo sde2): yang byed du 'dzud cing mthong ba dang / thos pa'i rjes su yi rang ba las byung ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / sems can gyi sgrib pa dang / chos kyi sgrib pa dang / don
169a4(mdo sde2): du smra ba la sgribs bsgribs par gyur to// 'di ltar tshig kyal pa yongs su spongs pa'i 'khor los lhag ma ma lus par yongs su spangs pa'i 'khor los lhag ma ma
169a5(mdo sde2): lus par yongs su bcom pas rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu mi len par byed do// lus 'di nyid la lha dang mi la sogs pa kun dga' zhing yid du 'ong bas dog pa med
169a6(mdo sde2): par 'gyur ba dang / lus dang sems rab du bde ba dang / tshig du smras pa thams cad don du 'gyur ba dang / 'chi 'pho ba'i dus byed pa na yang / lus dang sems la sdug
169a7(mdo sde2): bsngal gyis mi gdung zhing yid du 'ong ba'i bu dang chung ma dang 'khor gyis yongs su bskor bas 'chi 'pho ba'i yongs su bskor bas 'chi 'pho ba'i dus byed par 'gyur gyi/
169a8(mdo sde2): shin tu 'jigs pa'i gshin rje'i po nya mthong bar mi 'gyur ro// yid du 'ong ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen chos kyis dul ba tshul khrims dang yon tan du ldan pa bsod nas
169b1(mdo sde2): kyi zhing yang dag pa dang phrad de/ lus dang sems rab tu dga' ba dang de la bkur bsti dang bcas zhing shin tu dad pa skye bar 'gyur ro// tshe 'phos nas kyang phyir mi'i nang du
169b2(mdo sde2): skye zhing dbang po yongs su rdzogs pa yan lag dang ldan pa dang / gang nas gang du skyes par phan pa dang / don du 'gyur ba'i tshig smra ba dang / byad gzugs bzang ba dang /
169b3(mdo sde2): yid gzhungs pa dang / rab tu bde zhing skyid pa dang / phyir yang yid du 'ong ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen chos kyis dul ba tshul khrims dang yon tan du ldan pa/ bsod nams
169b4(mdo sde2): kyi zhing yang dag pa dang phrad de/ de'i rjes su slob pa dang / tshig kyal par smra ba yongs su spong ba dang / sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos thams cad yongs su gcod pa dang /
169b5(mdo sde2): dge ba'i chos khyad par can thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa dang / theg pa chen po'i chos kyi rnam grangs thams cad tshol ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam dang
169b6(mdo sde2): spyod pa thams cad la rim gyis gzhol zhing shin du yang ba'i ye shes kyis rgya mtsho la 'jug pa nas/ bla na med pa'i byang chub 'thob pa'i bar du 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi
169b7(mdo sde2): zhing na don med pa'i tshig thams cad bral te/ byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod du gtogs pa chos chen po'i sgra mchog dam pa rnams mang pos zhing de yongs su khyab pa dang /
169b8(mdo sde2): dpag tu med pa'i smon lam dang ye shes dam pa phun sum tshogs pas chos kyis don rnam pa sna tshogs 'chad pa la mkhas pa'i sems can de lta bu dag zhing der skye bar 'gyuraro//
170a1(mdo sde2): de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshe'i tshad kyang dpag tu med de/ sems can dag cis 'dul bzhin du dam pa'i chos ston to// yongs su mya ngan las
170a2(mdo sde2): 'das nas kyang / dam pa'i chos yun du gnas shing sems can tshad med pa la phan pa dang / bde ba'i don byed par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di ni byang chub sems
170a3(mdo sde2): dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i tshig kyal pa yongs su spong ba'i 'khor lo bdun pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'khor lo 'di dang ldan pas/
170a4(mdo sde2): nyan thos kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur/ nyan thos kyi theg pa'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med par
170a5(mdo sde2): 'gyur/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// theg pa chen po la 'khrul med par 'gyur/ theg pa chen po'i gang zag la 'khrul pa
170a6(mdo sde2): med par 'gyur ro// dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung yongs su 'phel ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la rab tu byung ba'i nye gnas chos kyi snod dam/ chos
170a7(mdo sde2): kyi snod ma yin pa yang rung / chung ngu na chos gos kyi tshal bu gyon cing sgra dang kha spu bregs pa la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur/ theg pa chen po'i chos gong nas gong du
170a8(mdo sde2): 'phar zhing phyir mi ldog pa dang / rno ba'i shes rab dang / bsod nams kyi khyad par rtag tu skye zhing 'phel ba dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / gzungs dang / bzod pa dang /
170b1(mdo sde2): sa rnams thams cad la dbang du 'gyur zhing phyir mi ldog pa dang / rtag tu dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang phrad cing de'i rjes su 'gro ba dang / rtag tu sangs rgyas thams
170b2(mdo sde2): cad mthong ba dang mi 'bral zhing byang chub sems dpa' dang nyan thos kyi nye gnas mthong ba dang mi 'bral dang / chos thos pa dang mi 'bral ba dang / dge 'dun la mchod
170b3(mdo sde2): pa dang / bsnyen bkur byed pa dang mi 'bral ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad la brtson pas sems mi ngoms pa dang / byang chub kyi spyod pa dang / smon lam rnam pa sna
170b4(mdo sde2): tshogs kyis sems mi ngoms 'gyur te/ 'bras bu gzhan thob pa yang ji skad bshad pa bzhin no// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
170b5(mdo sde2): chen po gang nam 'tsho'i bar du chags sems yongs su spangs na/ sems can thams cad kyis bkur zhing btsun par byed pa dang / sems rnam par dag cing rnyog
170b6(mdo sde2): ba dang bral te/ de'i dbang gis dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// thog ma med pa'i mtha' nas rgyud lngar 'khor bar 'khor ba'i rgya mtshor
170b7(mdo sde2): 'bying ba yang sems kyi dbang gis lus dang ngag yid sdig pa mi dge ba'i las bdag kyang byed la gzhan yang byed du 'dzud cing mthong ba dang / thos pas rje su yi rang
170b8(mdo sde2): ba las byung ba nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / sems can gyi sgrib pa dang / chos kyi sgrib pa dang / gnod sems med pa la sgribaso pas bsgribs par 'gyur ro//
171a1(mdo sde2): dadod sems yongs su spong ba'i 'khor los lhag ma ma lus par yongs su bcom pas rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu yongasu mi len te/
171a2(mdo sde2): lus 'di nyid la yang lha dang mi la sogs pa kun dga' zhing yid du 'ongs pa dang dogos pa med par 'gyur ba dang / lus dang sems rab du bde ba dang / sems
171a3(mdo sde2): rnam par dag cing chags pa med par 'gyur ro// 'chi 'pho ba'i dus byed pa na yang / lus dang sems la sdug bsngal gyis mi gdung ba dang / yid du 'ong ba'i
171a4(mdo sde2): bu dang chung ma dang 'khor gyis yongs su bskor pas 'chi 'pho ba'i dus byed par 'gyur gyi/ shin tu 'jig pa'i gshin rje'i pho nya mthong bar mi 'gyur ro// yid du
171a5(mdo sde2): 'ong ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen chos kyis dul ba tshul khrims dang yon tan du ldan pa bsod nams kyi zhing yang dag pa dang phrad de/ lus dang sems rab tu dga'
171a6(mdo sde2): ba dang / de la bkur sti dang bcas pas shin tu dad pa skye bar 'gyur ro// tshe 'phos nas kyang phyir mi'i nang du skye zhing dbang po yongs su rdzogs pa yan lag dang /
171a7(mdo sde2): ldan pa dang / gang nas gang du skyes pa der sems rnam par dag cing rnyog pa med pa dang / byad gzugs bzang ba dang / yid gzhungs pa dang / rab bde zhing skyid
171a8(mdo sde2): pa dang / phyir yang yid du 'ong ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen chos kyis dul ba tshul khrims dang yon tan du ldan pa/ bsod nams kyi zhing yang dag pa dang phrad de/
171b1(mdo sde2): de'i rjes su slob pa dang / chags sems yongs su spong ba dang / mi dge ba'i chos yongs su gcod pa dang / dge ba'i chos khyad par can thams cad yongs
171b2(mdo sde2): su rdzogs pa dang / theg pa chen po'i chos kyi rnam grangs thams cad tshol ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' smon lam dang spyod pa thams cad la rim gyis gzhol
171b3(mdo sde2): zhing / shin du yangs pa'i ye shes kyi rgya mtsho la 'jug pa nas/ bla na med pa'i byang chub 'thob pa'i bar du 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi zhing lag mthil bzhin du
171b4(mdo sde2): mnyam la/ rin po che rnam pa mang pos yongs su gang ba dang / rin po che'i shing rnam pa sna tshogs dkris pa dang / rin po che'i gos dang / rin po che'i rgyan gyi yo
171b5(mdo sde2): byad dang / rin po che'i rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / gdugs dang / gser dang / dngul dang / mu tig gi dra ba dang / shing la sogs pas yongs su gang ba dang /
171b6(mdo sde2): shin tu yid du 'ong zhing blta na sdug pa nga rgyal yongs su spangs pa byad gzugs shin tu mdzes pa dang / dbang po ma nyams pa sems ma nyams pa'i sems
171b7(mdo sde2): can dge zhing der skye bar 'gyur te/ chags sems med pa'i yon tan phun sum tshogs pas brgyan par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshe'i tshad
171b8(mdo sde2): kyang dpag tu med do// sems can dag cis 'dul ba bzhin du dam pa'i chos ston to// yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas kyang dam pa'i chos yun
172a1(mdo sde2): ring du gnas shing sems can tshad med pa la phan pa dang / bde ba'i don byed par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'
172a2(mdo sde2): sems dpa' chen po chags sems yongs su spangs pa'i 'khor lo brgyad pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'khor lo 'di dang ldan na/ nyan thos/
172a3(mdo sde2): kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur/ nyan thos kyi theg pa'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur/

172a8(mdo sde2): thams cad la dbang du 'gyur zhing phyir mi ldog pa dang / rtag tu dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang phrad cing rjes su 'thun par 'gyur ba dang rtag tu sangs rgyas thams cad
172b1(mdo sde2): mthong ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang nyan thos kyi nye gnas mthong ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / chos thos pa dang mi 'bral ba dang / dge 'dun la/

172b7(mdo sde2): rgya mtshor 'bying ba yang gnod sems kyi dbang gis lus dang ngag dang yid mi dge ba'i las bdag kyang byed la gzhan yang byed du 'dzud cing mthong ba dang / thos

173a1(mdo sde2): bsgribs par 'gyur to// 'di ltar gnod sems yongs su spangs pa'i 'khor los lhag ma ma lus par yongs su bcom pas rnam
173a2(mdo sde2): par smin pa'i 'bras bu yongasu mi len te/ lus 'di nyid la yang lha dang mi la sogs pa kun dga' zhing yid du 'ong ba dang / dogs pa mi 'gyur ba dang / sems

173a7(mdo sde2): dbang po yongs su rdzogs pa yan lag dang ldan pa gang ba dang gang du skyes par sems rnam par dag cing dri ma dang bral ba dang / byad gzugs bzang ba dang /

173b4(mdo sde2): pa'i bar du 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnyog pa dang / sme ba dang / sprin dang / khug rlangs dang / rdul dang dri ma dang / mi sdug pa mi mdzes pa thams cad dang
173b5(mdo sde2): bral te/ rin po che mang pos shin tu brgyan pa yid du 'ong ba dang / nga rgyal dang bral ba gzugs mdzes shing sdug pa dbang po me nyams pa sems rtag tu zhi ba'i
173b6(mdo sde2): sems can dag zhing der skyes te/ byams pa dang / snying rje dang / yon tan phun sum tshogs pas brgyan par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshe'i tshad kyang

174b7(mdo sde2): ba la sgrib pas bsgribs par 'gyur ro// 'di ltar log par lta ba yongs su spangs pa'i 'khor los lhag ma ma lus par bcom pas rnam par smin pa'i 'bras
174b8(mdo sde2): bu yongs su mi len te/ las 'di nyid la yang lha dang mi la sogs pa kun dga' zhing yid du 'ong ba dang dogs pa med par 'gyur ba dang / lus dang sems

175a6(mdo sde2): dang / rab tu bde zhing skyid pa dang / phyir yang yid du 'ong ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen chos kyis dul ba tshul khrims dang yon tan du ldan pa/ bsod nams zhing yang dag

175b1(mdo sde2): spyod pa thams cad rim gyis gzhol zhing shin tu yangs pa'i ye shes kyi rgya mtsho la 'jug pa nas/ bla na med pa'i byang chub 'thob pa'i bar du 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas
175b2(mdo sde2): kyi zhing nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa bral ba dang / lha'i bdud kyi 'khor thams cad dang bral ba dang / mu stegs can gyi 'khor thams cad dang bral ba
175b3(mdo sde2): dang / rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs kyis shin tu brgyan cing mdzes pa dang / yang dag par lta ba dang ldan zhing ngo mtshar dang / bkra shis dang tshul ngan pa'i lha
175b4(mdo sde2): ba sna tshogs dang / rtag par lta ba dang / chad par lta ba dang / bdag dang bdag gi bar lta ba thams cad yongs su spangs pa'i sems can dag zhing der skyes te/
175b5(mdo sde2): shin tu tshe ring ba dang / theg pa chen po'i ro gcig la yongs su spyod par 'gyur ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshe'i tshad kyang dpag tu med de sems can cis
175b6(mdo sde2): 'dul ba bzhin chos ston pa dang / yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas kyang dam pa'i chos yun ring du gnas shing sems can tshad med pa la phan pa dang / bde ba'i
175b7(mdo sde2): don tu ro gcig pa'i chos bstan pa la rtsod pa med pas yongs su rgyas par byed cing bgegs dang bar chad med par med par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'di ni
175b8(mdo sde2): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po log par lta ba yongs su spongs pa'i 'khor lo bcu pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'khor lo/
176a1(mdo sde2): rnam pa bcu po 'di dang ldan pas nyan thos kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// nyan thos kyi theg pa'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med
176a2(mdo sde2): par 'gyur ro// rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// theg pa chen
176a3(mdo sde2): po la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur/ theg pa chen po'i gang zag la 'khrul pa med par 'gyur ro// dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung yongs su 'phel ba dang / de bzhin
176a4(mdo sde2): gshegs pa'i bstan pa la rab tu byung ba'i nye gnas chos kyi snod dam/ chos kyi snod ma yin pa yang rung / chung ngu na chos gos kyi tshal bu gyon cing skra dang kha spu breg
176a5(mdo sde2): ba la 'khrul pa med pa dang / theg pa chen po'i chos la gong nas gong du 'phar zhing phyir mi ldog pa dang / rno ba'i shes rab dang / bsod nams kyi khyad par can rtag tu
176a6(mdo sde2): skye zhing 'phel ba dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / gzungs dang / bzod pa dang / sa rnams thams cad la dbang du 'gyur zhing phyir mi ldog pa dang / rtag tu dge ba'i bshes
176a7(mdo sde2): gnyen dang phrad cing rjes su slob pa dang / rtag tu sangs rgyas thams cad mthong ba dang mi 'bral zhing / byang chub sems dpa' dang nyan thos kyi nye gnas mthong ba
176a8(mdo sde2): dang mi 'bral ba dang / chos thos pa dang mi 'bral ba dang / dge 'dun la mchod pa dang bsnyen bkur byed pa dang mi 'bral ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad
176b1(mdo sde2): tshol ba la brtson pas sems mi ngoms pa dang / byang chub kyi spyod pa dang / smon lam dang pha rol tu phyin pa drug la sems mi ngoms par 'gyur te/ 'bras bu gzhan
176b2(mdo sde2): thob pa yang ji skad bshad pa bzhin no// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang 'khor lo rnam pa bcu po de dag ldan na myur du bla na med pa yang
176b3(mdo sde2): dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ snga ma 'das pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang
176b4(mdo sde2): dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyang mi dge ba bcu'i las yongs su spangs nas/ thams cad kyis dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam gyi sdug bsngal spangs
176b5(mdo sde2): shing sa stod de/ sems can thams cad la bde ba phan pa'i don dang / byang chub kyi lam skye zhing 'phel bar bya ba dang / sems can thams cad kyis las dang
176b6(mdo sde2): nyon mongs pa'i sdug bsngal lhag ma lus par bstsal bar bya ba dang / ngan song gsum bskam par bya ba dang / dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung bsab par bya ba
176b7(mdo sde2): dang / khams gsum gyi srid pa yongs su bskam par bya ba dang / phung po dang khams dang skye mched gcad par bya ba dang / thams cad myur du 'jigs pa/
176b8(mdo sde2): med pa'i mya ngan las 'da' ba'i grong khyer du gzud ba'i phyir ji skad bshad pa bzhin du mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi 'bras bu yongs su spong ngo // de bas na ri
177a1(mdo sde2): kyi bu gal te yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam 'di ma bsgrubs par mngon par 'tshang rgya ba 'am/ chung
177a2(mdo sde2): du na yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam 'ga' tsam yang mi srung bar nga ni theg pa chen po yang dag par spyod pa'o zhes 'am/ nga ni bla na
177a3(mdo sde2): med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub sgrub pa'o zhes zer na/ gang zag de ni shin tu brdzun par smra ste/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
177a4(mdo sde2): kyi spyan ngar 'jig rten slu ba dang / 'dzem pa dang ngo tsha ba med pa stong par smra zhing chad par lta ba glen pa mi shes pa slu ba can yin te de tshe 'phos nas ngan song du ltung
177a5(mdo sde2): par shes par bya'o// rigs kyi bu gang tshig tu brjod pa 'am/ mnyan pa tsam gyis chags ste dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bsgom pa 'am/ nan tan bya mi
177a6(mdo sde2): dgos par byang chub dang mya ngan las 'das pa thob tu zin na bskal pa cig la yud cig gis phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi sa'i khams
177a7(mdo sde2): kyi rdul phra mo snyed kyi sems can thams cad byang chub mngon par 'tshang rgya ste/ mya ngan las 'da' bar 'gyur ba zhig na/ de ni de lta bu'i gnas med do//
177a8(mdo sde2): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam ni theg pa chen po'i rtsa ba yin te/ byang chub kyi rgyu dang mya ngan las 'da' ba'i them skas lta bu'o// rigs kyi bu gal
177b1(mdo sde2): te sems bskyed pa tsam 'am smon lam btab pa tsam gyis mchog ste/ dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam goms par nan tan bya mi dgos par byang chub sems dpa'
177b2(mdo sde2): dang yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba 'thob tu zin na ni bskal pa gcig la yud tsam thang gcig gis phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi sa'i
177b3(mdo sde2): khams kyi rdul phra mo snyed kyi sems can yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya zhing mya ngan las 'da' bar 'gyur ba zhig na de ni de lta bu'i
177b4(mdo sde2): gnas med do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam ni 'jig rten las 'da' ba'i 'bras bu'i khyad par dang yon tan gyi rgyur 'gyur ro// rigs
177b5(mdo sde2): kyi bu gal te dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam la nan tan ma byas na/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul phra mo snyed kyi bskal par bdag ni theg pa
177b6(mdo sde2): chen po pa'o zhes zer te 'chad dam nyan tam/ sems skyed dam/ smon lam btab kyang / byang chub dang mya ngan las 'da' ba 'thob par mi 'gyur la gzhan yang
177b7(mdo sde2): 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal las 'don mi nus so// rigs kyi bu dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam la nan tan byed pas 'jig rten na rgyal rigs dang bram ze la sog
177b8(mdo sde2): pa rigs chen po dang / rgyal chen rigs bzhi'i lha nas 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched stengs kyi bar du yod pa dang / nyan thos kyi theg pa dang
178a1(mdo sde2): rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa dang / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub bar du yang yod par 'gyur te/ de dag kun kyang dge ba bcu'i
178a2(mdo sde2): las kyi lam la nan tan byed pa'i khyad par dang bye brag las gyur to// de bas na rigs kyi bu gang myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob par
178a3(mdo sde2): 'dod na/ dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam la nan tan gyis rgyun gyis brgyan te/ mi dge ba bcu'i sdom pa la mi gnas na bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
178a4(mdo sde2): tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// gang myur du theg pa chen po'i spyod yul chud par 'dod dam/ myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob par 'dod dam/
178a5(mdo sde2): myur du dge ba'i chos thams cad yongs su rdzogs par 'dod na/ sngar dge ba bcu'i lam shin tu bsrung bar bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ dge ba bcu'i las
178a6(mdo sde2): kyi lam gyis ni dge ba'i chos thams cad dang / yon tan rnam par gzhag pa'i gzhi dang / 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i 'bras bu mchog thob
178a7(mdo sde2): par byed pa'i rgyu yin no// de bas na dge ba bcu'i las la shin tu nan tan bya'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis don 'di dag gsal bar bzlas pa'i phyir tshig
178a8(mdo sde2): su bcad de gsung ba/ srid pa'i sdug bsngal kun gcod cing // byang chub chen po thob 'dod pa// dge bcu'i 'khor lo nan tan la// le lo ma byed brtson par gyis//
178b1(mdo sde2): theg pa gsum gyi dam chos dang // theg pa rnam gsum gang zag dang // rab tu byung ba thams cad la// 'khrul pa med par thob par 'gyur// theg chen spyod la
178b2(mdo sde2): dad mos shing // thams cad 'khor gyi dbyugs 'byin pa// chos mchog rtog nas zhing dag der// byang chub chen po myur du 'thob// gal te srog gcod yongs
178b3(mdo sde2): spangs na/ kun gyis kur zhing bla mar byed// rtag tu nad med tshe yang ring // bde zhing sgyid la gnod pa med// skye ba'i gnas ni thams cad du// sangs rgyas
178b4(mdo sde2): spyod yul lam la mos// sangs rgyas chos dang dge 'dun mthong // myur du bla med byang chub 'thob// ma byin len pa yongs spangs na// mkhas pas
178b5(mdo sde2): bkur zhing bla mar byed// 'dod chags skye ba'i lam kun zhe// 'dod chags med par skye bar 'gyur// skye ba kun tu longs spyod ldan// sbyin bdag chen
178b6(mdo sde2): por de 'gyur te// rin chen mang pos brgyan pa dang // yid 'ong sangs rgyas zhing yang 'thob/ 'dod pas log g.yem yongs spangs na// nyon mongs
178b7(mdo sde2): dri ma zhi bar 'gyur// 'dod chags sred pa'i rgya mtsho skye mas// rnam dag sangs rgyas zhing myur 'thob// sems can rnam pa mang po yang // 'dod pa'i
178b8(mdo sde2): 'dam las dgal bar 'gyur// theg chen la ni rab bkod nas// tshangs pa'i spyad pa spyod du btsud// brdzun du smras pa yongs spangs na// 'phags pa'i
179a1(mdo sde2): dbang dang ye shes 'thob// rtag tu bden la smra bar dga'// brdzun du 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal 'jil// tshig cig tshad mar/
179a2(mdo sde2): btsugs pas na// sangs rgyas chos dang dge 'dun mthong // brdzun mi smra ba bsgoms pas na// byang chub chen chen po myur du 'thob// phra ma'i tshig
179a3(mdo sde2): smra yongs spangs na// dge ba'i chos kyi snod du 'gyur// sangs rgyas chos dang dge 'dun mthong // chad par lta ba yongs mi 'gyur// 'phags pa'i
179a4(mdo sde2): chags med dga' ba dang // rin chen gser gyi gzungs 'thob cing // zab mo chos kyi rgya mtsho rig/ myur du bla med byang chub 'thob// gal te zhe gcod tshig spang te/

179a6(mdo sde2): ston par 'gyur// sangs rgyas mang po'i spyod yul shes// sa bcu las kyang 'da' bar 'gyur// kyal bar smra ba yongs spangs na// mkhas pas bkur zhing
179a7(mdo sde2): bla mar byed// gzhan la tshig du smra ba kun// yon tan rnam lnga 'thob par 'gyur// rtag tu 'phags pa'i tshig nyan cing // 'phags pa'i lam tshol spro bar 'gyur/
179a8(mdo sde2): sangs rgyas rgya mtsho yongs rdzogs shing // thams cad mkhyen pa myur du 'thob// gal te chags sems yongs spangs te// 'phags pa rnam la mi smod cing //
179b1(mdo sde2): ngur smrig gyon la mchod pa byed// theg pa gsum gyi byang chub sgrub// rtag tu rnam dag zhing du skye// ya ston pa'i gnas su gnas par 'gyur// bla med

179b3(mdo sde2): mnyam par bzhag pa'ang myur du 'thob// 'phags pa'i spyod yul mos par 'gyur// rnam dag sangs rgyas zhing du skye// nyes pa'i skyon rnams rnams
179b4(mdo sde2): kun dang bral// de la gnas na byang chub 'thob// gnod sems thams cad spang bar bya// ngan par lta ba yongs spangs te// rnam dag dad pa'i

181b6(mdo sde2): mi snyam pa'i bzod pa'i sems dang / sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal bya ba'i sems dang / sems can thams cad la bde ba'i sbyin
181b7(mdo sde2): pa'i sems dang / sems can thams cad mya ngan las bzla ba'i sems gnas te sbyin pa byed do// de bas na nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad las
181b8(mdo sde2): shin tu 'das pa/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing chen por 'gyur ba dang / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi zla ba thams//

182a3(mdo sde2): cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing yang dag pa zhes bya'o// gal te 'jig rten gyi 'dod pa rnam pa lnga yang ma spangs la/ byams dang snying rje chen po yang med par smin pa byin
182a4(mdo sde2): na/ sbyin pa'i dngos po tshad med dpag tu med pa gtang yang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po zhes mi bya ste/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi bsod

182a6(mdo sde2): dang snying rje chen po dang ldan pas sbyin pa bya'o// gal te 'jig rten gyi 'dod pa lnga yang ma spangs la/ byams pa dang snying rje chen po yang med par smin pa byed na/ byang chub
182a7(mdo sde2): sems dpa' zhes kyang mi bya la/ bsod nams kyi zhing yang dag pa ma yin no// rigs kyi bu 'dod pa rnam lnga la chags pas sbyin pa byed na bdag nyid kyi lus kyi sdug
182a8(mdo sde2): bsngal gyi cha chung zad kyang zhi bar 'gyur na/ sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal tshad med pa bstsal pa lta ci smos/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi don 'di dag gsal
182b1(mdo sde2): khar bzlas pa'i phyir tshigs su bcad de bka' stsal pa/ zang zing sbyin pa'i 'khor lo ldan pa// mkhas pa bsam pa dag pa'i mos pas// 'dod pa rnam pa lnga dag
182b2(mdo sde2): ni spangs te// sems can kun la phan pa bde byed// sems can kun la bde ba'i phyir gyi// rnam smin 'bras bu re phyir ma yin// sbyin pa'i dngos po byin pa chung
182b3(mdo sde2): yang // yang dag bsod nams zhing du de 'gyur// sbyin pa'i dngos po mang du byas kyang // 'dod pa rnam lnga dag la gnas na// 'phags pa dag gi phyag
182b4(mdo sde2): rgyas ma btag/ ma nges pa'i tshogs la gnas 'gyur// sbyin par bya ba'i dngos po chung yang // 'dod pa lnga la mi gnas pa ni// nyan thos dang rang sangs
182b5(mdo sde2): rgyal ba'i/ yang dag bsod nams zhing du du de 'gyur/ de bas 'dod pa rnam pa lnga spangs la/ rtag tu rnam dag sbyin byed cing / sems can kun la bde ba byas
182b6(mdo sde2): na// yang dag bsod nams zhing du de 'gyur// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos kyi sbyin pa'i go cha chen po'i 'khor
182b7(mdo sde2): lo rnam pa bcu yod de// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'khor lo de dang ldan na thog ma sems bskyed nas 'dod pa lnga yongs su gsal ba'i phyir/
182b8(mdo sde2): myur du nyi ma'i sgron me'i 'od ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob cing nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad las shin tu 'das pa/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas
183a1(mdo sde2): thams cad kyi bsod nams chen po'i zhing du 'gyur ba dang / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa thams cad kyis mchod pa
183a2(mdo sde2): dang bsrung ba dang bsnyen bkur bya bar 'gyur ro// bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis bstan pa dam pa'i chos nyan thos kyi theg pa dang ldan
183a3(mdo sde2): pa'i dam pa'i chos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa dang ldan pa'i chos dang / theg pa chen po dang ldan pa'i dam pa'i chos dang / 'jig rten gyi chos dang / 'jig
183a4(mdo sde2): rten las 'das pa'i chos dang / zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos dang / zag pa zad pa'i chos dang / 'dus byas kyi chos dang / 'dus ma byas kyi chos dang / gnyis
183a5(mdo sde2): su med pa'i chos rnams te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos rnam pa bcu po 'di la dad cing // gus par byed pa dang / ji skad thob pa'i rnams
183a6(mdo sde2): ji nus su gzungs su 'dzin cing yid la byed do// rab tu rtog go/ mthar khong du chud par byed cing / gzhan dag la yang ci rigs par ston par byed do// nam
183a7(mdo sde2): chos ston pa'i tshe na phra dog med pa'i sems dang / ser sna med pa'i sems dang / nga rgyal med pa'i sems dang / rnyed pa med pa'i sems dang / gzhan gyi mi smod
183a8(mdo sde2): pa'i sems dang / bdag mi stod pa'i sems dang / sti stang bcas pa'i sems dang / byams pa chen po'i sems dang / snying rje chen po'i sems su bya'o//
183b1(mdo sde2): nyan thos kyi theg pa can gyi gang zag la ni nyan thos kyi thos chos ston cing 'chad de/ de la rang sangs rgyas kyi chos sam/ theg pa chen po'i chos kyi ma yin/
183b2(mdo sde2): pa dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa can gyi gang zag la ni/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i chos ston gyi/ nyan thos kyi theg pa'i chos sam/ theg pa chen pi
183b3(mdo sde2): chos kyis ma yin pa dang / theg pa chen po'i gang zag la ni theg pa chen po'i chos kyi ston gyi/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i chos kyis ma yin
183b4(mdo sde2): pa dang / sems can gyi dbang po dang snod ji lta bu bzhin du dam pa'i chos sngon gyi dbang po dang snod du ma gyur pa la chos mi ston to// gang theg pa chen po
183b5(mdo sde2): sems can la rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa spyod cig par ram/ nyan thos kyi theg pa spyod cig par mi skul lo// rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa can gyi
183b6(mdo sde2): sems can la skabs kha cig tu theg pa chen po la nan tan byos shig ces skul ba'i skabs ni yod do// nyan thos kyi theg pa can gyi sems can la skab
183b7(mdo sde2): kha cig tu rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i spyod pa dang / theg pa chen po'i spyod pa la nan tan gyi shig ces skul ba'i skabs kyang yod de/ de bzhin gshegs
183b8(mdo sde2): pas bstan pa'i dam pa'i chos chung ngu na tshigs su bcad pa gcig gam/ tshigs su bcad pa phyed tsam la yang shin tu dad cing bkur ste byed kyi de la
184a1(mdo sde2): 'phya ba 'am/ bskur ba 'am/ bgegs sam bar chad mi byed de/ chos ston pa la sangs rgyas dang 'dra bar 'du shes pa dang /
184a2(mdo sde2): chos nyan pa'i 'khor rnams la nad pa dang 'dra bar 'du shes pa dang / gang 'chad pa'i chos rnams la sman bzang po dang 'dra bar 'du shes shing / 'dod pa kwa rnam
184a3(mdo sde2): lnga yongs su bcad de/ re ba med pas dam pa'i chos ston to// rigs kyi bu 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i chos kyi sbyin pa go cha chen
184a4(mdo sde2): po'i 'khor lo rnam pa bcu zhes bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang 'khor lo de dang ldan na 'dod pa lnga yongs su bskul te/ myur du nyi ma'i
184a5(mdo sde2): sgron me'i 'od ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob cing / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad las shin tu 'das pa dang / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi
184a6(mdo sde2): bsod nams kyi zhing du 'gyur ba dang / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa thams cad kyis mchod pa dang bsrung ba dang bsnyen bkur byed par 'gyur ro// de nas
184a7(mdo sde2): bcom ldan 'das kyis don 'di dag gsal bar bzlas pa'i phyir tshigs su bcad de bka' stsal pa/ mkhas pa chos kyi sbyin pa spyod pa dag/ snod bzhin theg pa gsum gyi
184a8(mdo sde2): chos ston te// theg pa gzhan dag de la ston mi byed// thos nas de la 'phya zhing skur mi 'gyur// dbang po snod bzhin dam pa'i chos ston gyi// dbang po snod min dag
184b1(mdo sde2): la ma yin no// so sor ji ltar ci la mos pa bzhin// de dang de'i chos ston mgu bar byed// theg pa chen po spyod pa'i gang zag la// theg pa rnam pa gnyis
184b2(mdo sde2): kyi chos mi bstan// bar bar theg pa gnyis kyi gang zag la// theg pa gnyis 'bring dang rab kyi chos ston to// shin tu dad cing gus par chos mnyan gyi//
184b3(mdo sde2): de la 'phya zhing bskur bar mi bya'o// chos smra ba la mchod pa byed pa ni// sangs rgyas 'dra bar de 'du shes bskyed// kun nas nyon mongs pa'i nad bsal phyir//
184b4(mdo sde2): dam pa'i chos kyi smon dag nyan par bskul// khe dang grags pa shin tu ring spangs te// dam pa'i chos dag bstan cing bshad par bya// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang
184b5(mdo sde2): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i tshul khrims rnam par dag pa'i go cha chen po'i 'khor lo yod de// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang
184b6(mdo sde2): 'khor lo de dang ldan na/ thog ma sems bskyed nas 'dod pa lnga yongs su gsal te/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad las shin tu 'das pa/ nyan
184b7(mdo sde2): thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing chen por 'gyur ba dang / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa thams cad kyis mchod pa dang
184b8(mdo sde2): bsrung ba dang bsnyen bkur bya bar 'gyur ro// de la ji ltar na/ tshul khrims rnam par dag pa go cha chen po'i 'khor lo zhe na/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa'i tshul
185a1(mdo sde2): khrims rnam par dag pa rnam pa gnyis te/ thun mong ba dang thun mong ma yin no// de la ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrim
185a2(mdo sde2): rnam par dag pa'i 'khor lo can thun mong ba zhe na/ khang khyim na gnas pa dge bsnyen pa dang / dge bsnyen ma'i tshul khrims kyi sdom pa blangs pa 'am/ yang na rab tu
185a3(mdo sde2): byang ba so sor thar pa'i tshul khrims kyis bsnyen par rdzogs pa ste/ sdom pa 'di dang so sor thar pa'i tshul khrims 'di ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims
185a4(mdo sde2): rnam par dag pa'i 'khor lo thun mong ba ste/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad dang thun mong ba yin no// byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims kyi 'khor
185a5(mdo sde2): lo rnam par dag pa 'di'i dbang gis sems can thams cad kyi kun nas nyon mongs pa chod par ram/ log par lta ba sel bar ram/ las kyi sgrib pa dang
185a6(mdo sde2): 'khor ba las grol bar mi 'gyur te/ go cha chen po'i 'khor lo zhes kyang mi bya/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po zhes kyang mi bya ste/ nyan thos
185a7(mdo sde2): dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing yang dag pa yang ma yin no// de la ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims rnam par dag pa go cha chen
185a8(mdo sde2): po'i thun mong ma yin zhe na/ gang byang chub sems dpa' rnams phyogs bcu'i sems can thams cad la mnyam pa nyid kyi sems dang / gnod pa med pa'i sems dang /
185b1(mdo sde2): khon tu 'dzin pa med pa'i sems kyis rnam par dag pa'i tshul khrims srung ngo // tshul khrims dang / tshul khrims ngan pa dang / sbyid pa dang / ser sna dang / byams pa dang /
185b2(mdo sde2): zhe sdang dang / brtson 'grus dang le lo can rab 'bring ba ma kun la bye brag mi 'byed pa'i sems dang / khyad par med pa'i 'du shes kyis tshul khrims yongs su srung ngo //
185b3(mdo sde2): khams gsum gyi sems can thams cad zhe sdang med pa dang / khong khro ba med pa dang / ngan par spyod pa med pas tshul khrims yongs su srung ngo // srid pa gsum gyi
185b4(mdo sde2): phung po dang khams dang skye mched la rnam par rtog pa med pas tshul khrums yongs su spong ngo // 'dod pa'i khams la mi gnas par tshul khrims srung ngo // gzugs yod
185b5(mdo sde2): pa'i khams la mi gnas par tshul khrims srung ngo // gzugs med pa'i khams la mi gnas par tshul khrims srung ngo // srid pa'i rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu thams
185b6(mdo sde2): cad la mi gnas par tshul khrims srung ngo // rnyed pa dang mi rnyed pa la mi gnas par tshul khrims srung ngo // 'du byed rnams la mi gnas par tshul khrims srung ste/
185b7(mdo sde2): 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims rnam par dag pa go cha chen po'i 'khor lo thun mong ma yin pa zhes bya'o// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' sems
185b8(mdo sde2): dpa' chen po gang tshul khrims rnam par dag pa po mchen po'i 'khor lo 'di dang ldan na ga ma semaso bskyed nas/ 'dod po lnga yongs su bskul te/

186a3(mdo sde2): bsrung ba dang bsnyen bkur bya bar 'gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis don 'di dag gsal bar bzlas pas phyi'i tshigs su bcad de bka' sprul pa/
186a4(mdo sde2): khyim na gnas shing sdod pa len pa// rang 'byung so sor thar pa'i tshul khrims// theg pa gnyis dang thun mong yin te// byang chub chen po zhes ni mi bya/
186a5(mdo sde2): mkhas pa stong pa nyid chos bsgom pa// 'jig rten kun la mi rten mi gnas// srid pa kun la gnas ma yin par// rnam par dag pa'i tshul khrims srung ngo //
186a6(mdo sde2): mtshan ma spong ba'i tshul khrims dag ni// chags pa med de zag pa kun med// tshul khrims 'di ltar srung ba dag ni// yang dag bsod nams zhing zhes de bya//
186a7(mdo sde2): rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' chen po bzod pa'i go cha'i 'khor lo chen po zhes bya ba yod de/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang 'khor

186b3(mdo sde2): gang zhe na/ 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'o// de la ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa'i 'jig rten pa'i bzod pa gang zhe na/ de ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i
186b4(mdo sde2): bzod pa ste/ sems can la dmigs pa len pa dang bcas pa'i mtshan ma dang bcas rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu la rten pa/ bsod nams kyi las la rten te//
186b5(mdo sde2): bzod par byed pa'o// gzhan yang bdag gi gzugs dang / sgra dang dri dang / ro dang reg bya la rten nas bzod par byed do// 'jug pa dang bcas pa'i
186b6(mdo sde2): bzod pa ji mi snyam pa med pa'i bzod pa dang / mthu zhan pa'i bzod pa'i sems can gtong ba'i bzod pa dang / g.yo dang rgyur bcas pa'i bzod pa dang / pha
186b7(mdo sde2): rol la 'dri ba'i bzod pa dang / sems can la phan pa dang / bde ba'i don mi byed pa'i bzod pa ste/ 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa'i 'jig rten gyi bzod pa
186b8(mdo sde2): zhes bya ste/ bzod pa 'di ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas las sogs pa dang / thun mong ba ma yin gyi go cha chen po'i 'khor lo zhes mi bya'o// de la ji ltar na

187a3(mdo sde2): 'phags pa thams cad kyi chos chen po'i 'od kyis sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i don gyi phyir chags pa med pa'i bzod pa dang bya ba'i dngos po thams
187a4(mdo sde2): cad dang tshig tu smra ba dang / rgyu dang mtshan ma dang / yi ge dang sgra dang skad thams cad yongs su bcad pa'i skye mched la rten pa'i bzod pa spyod do// bzod pa 'di
187a5(mdo sde2): bsgoms pas kun nas nyon mongs pa gsum dang / bskal pa rnams gsum dang / mtshan nyid gsum dang / dus gsum dang / srid pa gsum dang / 'du byed

187a7(mdo sde2): su bcad pas/ bzod pa 'di bsgom pa'i tshe/ sems dang yid rab tu zhi bas 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i 'jig rten las 'das pa'i go cha chen po'i 'khor lo'i bzod

187b6(mdo sde2): phyin ci logs pa rnam bzhi bstsal nas/ chags pa med pa'i bzod pa sgom zhing / 'du byed rnam pa gsum dag zhi na/ bzod pa 'di la thams cad bstod
187b7(mdo sde2): 'gyur/ 'du byed thams cad rab tu ni zhing / rtog pa thams cad yongs su spangs te/ sems ni nam mkha' 'dra bar mnyam pa/ bzod pa 'di la rnams/

188a1(mdo sde2): ni phan yon che 'gyur/ rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i brtson 'grus kyi go cha chen po'i

188a6(mdo sde2): sems dpa'i 'jig rten pa'i brtson 'grus shes na/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams shin tu 'bad pa'i brtson 'grus kyis 'jig rten gyi bsod nams kyi las
188a7(mdo sde2): kyi dngos po rnam pa gsum la nan tan byed do// gsum gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sbyin pa byed pa'i bsod nams kyi las dang / tshul khrims bsrung ba'i bsod nams
188a8(mdo sde2): kyi las dang / bsgom pa'i bsod nams byed pa'i las so// las 'di dag byed pa na brtson 'grus rnam pa gsum zhes bya ste/ brtson 'grus rnam pa 'di dag ni sems
188b1(mdo sde2): can la dmigs pa'i zag pa dang bcas pa nye bar len pa dang bcas pa/ rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu la rten pa bsod nams kyi las dang rten pa ste/ de ni byang

188b7(mdo sde2): dang sbyin pa dang ser sna dang / tshul khrims dang / ngan pa'i tshul khrims can dang / byams pa dang / zhe sdang dang / sems can rab dang 'bring dang / za ma
188b8(mdo sde2): kun la mi 'byed pa'i sems dang / bye brag med pa'i 'du shes kyis shin tu 'bad pa'i brtson 'grus brtsom mo// khams gsum gyi sems can thams cad
189a1(mdo sde2): la mnyam pa nyid dang / dmigs pa med pas bya ba'i las byed de/ smra ba dang rtog pa dang / dpyod pa'i gnas thams cad la mi
189a2(mdo sde2): gnas pa'i sems kyis shin tu 'bad pa'i brtson 'grus rtsom mo// srid pa gsum gyi phung po dang / khams dang skye mched la rnam par rtog pa med pas shin tu 'bad
189a3(mdo sde2): ba'i 'urtson 'grus rtsom ste/ 'dod pa'i khams la mi gnas pa'i 'bad pa med pa'i brtson 'grus dang / gzugs yod pa'i khams la mi gnas pa'i 'bad pa'i
189a4(mdo sde2): brtson 'grus dang / gzugs med pa'i khams la mi gnas pa'i 'bad pa'i brtson 'grus dang / srid pa'i rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu thams cad la mi rtog pa'i
189a5(mdo sde2): brjod 'grus dang / rnyed pa dang ma rnyed pa kun la mi gnas pa'i 'bad pa'i brtson 'grus dang / 'du byed rnams la mi gnas pa'i 'bad pa'i brtson 'grus dang / 'jig
189a6(mdo sde2): rten gyi bsod nams kyi las dang dngos po gsum mi gnas pa'i 'bad pa'i brtson 'grus dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa dang ldan pa'i bsod nams kyi las kyi dngos po
189a7(mdo sde2): rnam pa gsum la mi gnas pa'i 'bad pa'i brtson 'grus dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa dang ldan pa'i bsod nams kyi las kyi dngos po rnam pa gsum la shin tu
189a8(mdo sde2): brtson 'grus brtsom pa ste/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i 'jig rten las 'das pa'i brtson 'grus kyi go cha chen po'i 'khor lo zhes bya'o// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems
189b1(mdo sde2): dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang brtson 'grus kyi go cha chen po'i 'khor lo de dang ldan na/ thog ma sems bskyed pa nas/ 'dod pa rnam pa lnga yongs su bsngal te/ byang chub
189b2(mdo sde2): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po zhes bya'o// nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad las shin tu 'das te/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsod
189b3(mdo sde2): nams kyi zhing du 'gyur ba dang / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas theg pa pa thams cad kyis mchod pa dang / bsrungs pa dang bsnyen bkur byed par 'gyur ro// de nas
189b4(mdo sde2): bcom ldan 'das kyis don 'di dag gsal bar bzlas pa'i phyir tshigs su bcad de bka' stsal pa/ dngos po drug la shin tu chags pa'i// bus pa chu bo lngas ni
189b5(mdo sde2): khyer ba// shin tu 'bad pa'i brtson 'grus rtsom yang // mkhas pa rnams kyis de la smod 'gyur// sems can dmigs shing zad pa dang bcas la// len
189b6(mdo sde2): par bcas cing brtson 'grus rtsom na// yang dag bsod nams zhing ma yin te// byang chub sems dpa' chen po ma yin// mkhas pa brtson 'grus rtsom
189b7(mdo sde2): pa dag ni// chags pa thams cad ring du spangs te// sems ni ci la'ang mi gnas mi tshogs// yang dag bsod nams zhing zhes bya// ming dang gzugs la/
189b8(mdo sde2): chags pa med cing // phung po dang khams dang skye mched te// thams cad 'khor gyi rten du 'gyur ba// de ni byang chub sems dpa' chen po// 'jig
190a1(mdo sde2): rten spyod kyang chu zla bzhin te// 'bad pa'i brtson 'grus rtsom pa'i mthar phyin// 'khor lo 'dis yis yongs su bcom pa//
190a2(mdo sde2): skye bo'i kun nas nyon mongs bcings pa'o// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i bsam gtan gyi go cha chen po'i 'khor lo
190a3(mdo sde2): yod de/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang 'khor lo 'di dang ldan na thog ma sems bskyed pa nas/ 'dod pa lnga yongs su bstsal te/
190a4(mdo sde2): nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad las shin tu 'das nas/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing chen por 'gyur ba dang /
190a5(mdo sde2): nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa thams cad kyis mchod pa dang bsrung ba dang / bsnyen bkur byed par 'gyur ro// de la ji ltar na bsam gtan gyi tshe chen
190a6(mdo sde2): be'i 'khor lo zhe na/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa'i bsam gtan la rnam pa gnyis te/ 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'o// de la ji ltar na
190a7(mdo sde2): byang chub sems dpa'i 'jig rten gyi bsam gtan zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams phung po la gnas nas/ bsam gtan sgom pa dang / khams la gnas
190a8(mdo sde2): nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / skye mched la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / 'dod pa'i khams la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / gzugs
190b1(mdo sde2): yod pa'i khams la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / gzugs med pa'i khams la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / sdom pa gsum la gnas nas bsam/
190b2(mdo sde2): gtan sgom pa dang / rnam par grol ba gsum la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / yang
190b3(mdo sde2): dag par spong ba bzhi la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / dbang po lnga la gnas nas bsam
190b4(mdo sde2): gtan sgom pa dang / stobs lnga la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / byang chub kyi yan lag bdun la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / 'phags pa'i
190b5(mdo sde2): lam yan lag brgyad pa la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / sa'i khams la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom dang / chu'i khams la gnas nas bsam gtan
190b6(mdo sde2): sgom pa dang / me'i khams la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / rlung gi khams la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / nam mkha'i khams la gnas
190b7(mdo sde2): nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / rnam par shes pa'i khams la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / bde bar che ba la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang /
190b8(mdo sde2): sdug bsngal ba'i tshor ba la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / bde ba yang ma yin sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa'i tshor ba la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang /
191a1(mdo sde2): nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched la gnas nas bsam/
191a2(mdo sde2): gtan sgom pa dang / chung zad med min skye mched gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa
191a3(mdo sde2): dang / 'jig rten 'di la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / 'jig rten pha rol la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / 'du shes chung ngu la gnas nas
191a4(mdo sde2): bsam gtan sgom pa dang / 'du shes chen po la gnas nas bsam gtan sgom pa dang / 'du shes tshad med pa la gnas nas bsam gtan slob pa
191a5(mdo sde2): dang / bsam gtan de dag zag pa dang bcas pa/ nye bar len pa dang bcas pa/ chags pa dang bcas pa ste/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'
191a6(mdo sde2): chen po'i 'jig rten dang bcas pa'i bsam gtan zhes bya'o// bsam gtan 'di ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa dang thun mong ba zhes bya ste/ go cha chen po'i
191a7(mdo sde2): 'khor lo ma yin/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po zhes mi bya ste/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing yang dag pa ma yin no//
191a8(mdo sde2): de la ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'i 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bsam gtan zhe na 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams phung po dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang /
191b1(mdo sde2): khams dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / skye mched dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / 'dod pa'i khams dang bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang /
191b2(mdo sde2): gzugs kyi khams dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / gzugs med pa'i khams dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / sdom pa gsum dang bral
191b3(mdo sde2): bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / rnam par thar pa gsum dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi dang bral bar bsam gtan
191b4(mdo sde2): sgom pa dang / yang dag par spong ba bzhi dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang /
191b5(mdo sde2): dbang po lnga dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / stobs lnga dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / byang chub kyi yan lag
191b6(mdo sde2): bdun dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / sa'i khams dang bral bar
191b7(mdo sde2): bsam gtan sgom pa dang / chu'i khams dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / me'i khams dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / rlung gi khams
191b8(mdo sde2): dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / nam mkha'i khams dang bral bar bsam gtan bsgom pa dang / rnam par shes pa'i khams dang bral bar bsam
192a1(mdo sde2): gtan sgom pa dang / bde bar tshor ba dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / sdug bsngal tshor ba dang bral bar bsam gtan
192a2(mdo sde2): sgom pa dang / sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin par tshor ba dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched dang bral
192a3(mdo sde2): bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / cung zad med min skye mched dang bral bar bsam
192a4(mdo sde2): gtan sgom pa dang / 'du shes med min skye mched dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / 'jig rten 'di dang bral bar bsam gtan skom pa dang / 'jig rten/
192a5(mdo sde2): pha rol dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / 'du shes chung ngu dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / 'du shes chen po dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom
192a6(mdo sde2): pa dang / 'du shes tshad med pa dang bral bar bsam gtan sgom pa dang / bsam gtan 'di ni 'phags pa'i 'od gzer chen po skyed pa zag bla med pa/ nye bar
192a7(mdo sde2): len pa med pa/ chags pa med pa ste/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i 'jig rten las 'da' ba'i bsam gtan gyi gi che chen po'i 'khor lo zhes bya'o//
192a8(mdo sde2): rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang bsam gtan gyi go cha chen po'i 'khor lo 'di dang ldan na/ thog ma sems bskyed pa nas/
192b1(mdo sde2): 'dod pa lnga yongs su bstsal te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po zhes bya'o// nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad las shin tu 'das shing //
192b2(mdo sde2): nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing du 'gyur ba dang / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa thams cad kyis mchod pa dang /
192b3(mdo sde2): bsrung ba dang bsnyen bkur byed par 'gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis don 'di dag gsal bar bzlas pa'i phyir tshigs su bcad de bka' stsal pa/
192b4(mdo sde2): bdag gi khur lci spong ba'i phyir ni/ dmigs dang bcas pa'i ting nge 'dzin sgom ste/ bdag gi kun nas nyon mongs gcod 'dod/ yang dag mkhas pa'i mtshan
192b5(mdo sde2): nyid ma yin/ snod la rten cing rtog dang bcas pa/ rnam par grol 'dod ting 'dzin sgom yang / tshul rol pha rol mu la gnas na/ sems can dag la phan
192b6(mdo sde2): don byed min/ sems can kun la phan dang bde phyir/ ting 'dzin sgom zhing khur lci spong ste/ kun nas nyon mongs thams cad sel ba/ de ni yang dag
192b7(mdo sde2): mkhas pa'i mtshan nyid/ sems can thams cad sim par byed phyir/ mi gnas pa'i ting 'dzin sgom ste/ 'dod pa'i srid pa thams cad gcod pa/
192b8(mdo sde2): de ni blo gros chen po zhes bya/ srid pas bcings pa thams cad bkrol te/ 'jigs pa med pa'i grol du gzung phyir/ rab tu zhi ba'i ting 'dzin sgom pa/ de ni
193a1(mdo sde2): byang chub sems dpa' chen po'o// // bam po bcu pa'o//
193a2(mdo sde2): rigs kyi bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi go cha chen po'i 'khor lo zhes bya ba yod de/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'

193a6(mdo sde2): la ni rnam pa gnyis te/ 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'o// de la ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa'i 'jig rten pa'i shes rab ce na/ 'di lta ste
193a7(mdo sde2): byang chub sems dpa' rnams theg pa gsum gyi dam pa'i chos klog pa dang / 'don pa dang / glegs bam du 'dri ba dang / nyan pa dang / pha rol la ston cing 'chad
193a8(mdo sde2): po 'ba' shig la rten te/ sems can thams cad kyis ma rig pa'i mun pa sel bar 'dod pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi shes rab kyi sgron ma dbyung
193b1(mdo sde2): pa'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pas bstan pI'i// nyan thos kyi theg pa dang ldan pa'i chos la shin tu 'bad pa'i brtson 'grus kyis klog pa dang / 'don pa dang
193b2(mdo sde2): nyan pa dang / glegs bam du 'dri ba dang / gzhan dag la rgyas par ston cing 'chad pa dang / yang dag pa'i brtson 'grus kyis nan tan byed pa dang /
193b3(mdo sde2): de bzhin gshegs pas bstan pa'i rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa dang ldan pa'i chos la klog pa dang / 'don pa dang / nyan pa dang / glegs bam du 'dri ba
193b4(mdo sde2): dang / gzhan dag la ston cing 'chad pa dang / yang dag pa'i brtson 'grus kyis nan tan du spyod do// de bzhin gshegs pas bstan pa'i theg pa
193b5(mdo sde2): chen po dang ldan pa'i chos la brtson 'grus su glog pa dang / 'don pa dang / nyan pa dang glegs du 'dri ba dang / gzhan dag la yang rgyas par ston
193b6(mdo sde2): cing 'chad pa dang / yang dag pa'i brtson 'grus kyis nan tan byed pa ste/ 'phags pa'i zag pa med pa'i lam gyi yan lag tshol ba ma yin//
193b7(mdo sde2): 'phags pa'i lam du gtogs rnam par grol ba'i tshor ba la ma yin/ rab tu zhi ba yang dag pa'i shes rab la nan tan byed pa ma yin te/ rtag
193b8(mdo sde2): tu lta ba dang bcas pa mtshan ma dang bcas pa'i shes rab la nan tan byed do// de ltar len pa dang bcas pa/ chags pa dang bcas pa'i shes rab ni byang

194a6(mdo sde2): mi g.yo ba dang / mi rtog pa dang / ngo bo nyid med pa dang / nam mkha' lta bu'i sems dang / rab tu zhi ba'i sems dang / 'phel ba dang 'grib pa med
194a7(mdo sde2): pa'i shes rab dang / chags pa med pa'i sems dang / skye ba dang 'grog pa med pa'i sems dang / phyir mi ldog pa'i sems dang / chos mnyam pa nyid
194a8(mdo sde2): kyi sems dang / de bzhin nyid kyi sems dang / yang dge ba'i mtha'i sems dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi cha sems dang / bdag med pa'i sems dang /
194b1(mdo sde2): rnam par mi rtog pa'i sems dang / rab tu zhi ba dang bzod pa dang / rtog pa dang bral ba'i sems kyis grub pa dang / 'jig pa med pa'i se la shin tu
194b2(mdo sde2): thabs mkhas pas bde bar gnas pa dang / mi gnas pa/ mi chags pa'i mchog dam pa'i blo gros sa la thabs mkhas pas bde bar gnas pa ste/

195b1(mdo sde2): nyan thos kyi theg pa dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa dang / theg pa chen po'i snod ma yin pa nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi dbang po yongs su mi smin
195b2(mdo sde2): pa la shin tu phra la zab pa dam pa'i chos ston te/ slob du bzhug pa dang / 'phags pa'i bsam gtan la nan tan byed du gzhug go// gzhan yang don dam
195b3(mdo sde2): pa'i bden pa bstan te/ nan tan byed du gzhug pa dang / phyin ci log bzhi las bzla zhing mi ltung ba'i chos kyi mtshan nyid rig par bya ba dang / so so yang

195b6(mdo sde2): ma lus pa'i lam dang / lam gyi 'bras bu'i bar du 'jug par bya ba mkhas pa'i ye shes kyis yongs su smin par byed do// sems san gang khe dang
195b7(mdo sde2): grags pa dang / longs spyod la chags te dbang po rgod pa dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su ma smin pa la ni mdo sde dang / 'dul ba dang / mang mo klog pa dang 'don byed
195b8(mdo sde2): du gzhug pa dang / sangs rgyas gzhan gyis bshad pa las gzhan pa rnam par grol ba dang / 'dun pa'i gtsug lag klog cing 'don du bcug te/ yongasu

196b5(mdo sde2): mkhas pa la 'ang mi sa rten dge ba'i bshes gnyen la'ang mi ltos par 'jig rten ma thabs mkhas pa la nan tan byed na/ byang chub sems dpa'i de ni 'jig rten
196b6(mdo sde2): gyi thams mkhas pas rmongs pa yin te/ ngan song du ltung bar 'gyur ro// de ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shin tu thabs mkhas pA la ye shes la gzhol zhing gnas

196b8(mdo sde2): par yang mi shes la/ shin tu thabs mkhas pa la'ang rmongs par gyur pas/ nyan thos kyi theg pa dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa dang / theg pa
197a1(mdo sde2): chen po'i snod ma yin pa dang / theg pa chen po'i dbang por ma smin pa dag la theg pa chen po ston pa dang / slob cing nan tan byed du
197a2(mdo sde2): bcug go// gang theg pa chen po'i chos kyi snod du gyur pa'i sems can la ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i chos ston cing nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg
197a3(mdo sde2): pa la slob cing nan tan byed du bcug go// gang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i chos kyi snod du gyur pa'i sems can la ni nyan thos kyi theg pa'i chos ston cing / nyan thos kyi

197a6(mdo sde2): bzhin du log par lta ba'i bar du mos pa dag la ni shin tu thabs mkhas pa la mongs pas zab pa chen po'i chos ston te/ de la 'khor ba 'di nas shi 'phos nas pa

198b2(mdo sde2): yang dag pa stan te/ khyad kyis slob du 'jug go// sems can gang sbyin pa la mos par gyur pa rnams la ni tshul khrims rnam par dag pa'i mchog srung ba ston pa dang
198b3(mdo sde2): de bzhin du/ rgyas par sems can gang bsam gtan la mos par gyur pa la ni zag pa med / pa/ 'phags pa'i lam gyi mchog gis bsdus pa dang / shes rab bla na med/
